<script>
function copySnowbotCode(event, element) {
    event.preventDefault(); 
    event.stopPropagation(); 
    
    const code = "VENTEKAMAS";
    
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(code).then(function() {
        const textSpan = element.querySelector('.snowbot-badge-copy-text');
        const originalText = textSpan.innerText;
        
        textSpan.innerText = "COPIÉ !";
        textSpan.style.color = "#22c55e";
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            textSpan.innerText = originalText;
            textSpan.style.color = "#3b5998";
        }, 2000);

    }, function(err) {
        console.error('Erreur copie :', err);
    });
}
</script>

 	<li>SEPA: Paiement instantane après la livraison des kamas.</li>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                // Define form IDs and messages
                var forms = {
                    2: {
                        message: "Vous devez être connecté pour vendre",
                        alert: "Vous devez être connecté pour soumettre votre commande."
                    },
                    13: {
                        message: "Vous devez être connecté pour vendre",
                        alert: "Vous devez être connecté pour soumettre votre commande."
                    },
                    10: {
                        message: "Vous devez être connecté pour échanger",
                        alert: "Vous devez être connecté pour soumettre votre commande."
                    }
                };

                for (var formId in forms) {
                    var form = document.getElementById('frm_form_' + formId + '_container');
                    if (form) {
                        var submitButton = form.querySelector('input[type="submit"], button[type="submit"]');
                        if (submitButton) {
                            submitButton.disabled = true;
                            submitButton.value = forms[formId].message;
                            submitButton.innerText = forms[formId].message;

                            // Add an event listener to prevent form submission
                            form.addEventListener('submit', function(event) {
                                event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                                event.preventDefault();
                                alert(forms[formId].alert);
                                return false;
                            });
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        </script>
            <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            // Function to replace text globally on the page
            function replaceTextContent(searchText, replaceText) {
                // Get all text nodes on the page
                var walker = document.createTreeWalker(
                    document.body,
                    NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT,
                    null,
                    false
                );

                // Loop through each text node
                var node;
                while (node = walker.nextNode()) {
                    // Check if the text node contains the search text
                    if (node.nodeValue.includes(searchText)) {
                        // Replace the search text with the replacement text
                        node.nodeValue = node.nodeValue.replace(searchText, replaceText);
                    }
                }
            }

            // Check if we're on the specific pages
            var currentURL = window.location.href;

            // For English pages
			if (
				currentURL.includes('/eng/vendre-des-kamas') ||
				currentURL.includes('/eng/echange-kamas/') ||
				currentURL.includes('/vendre-compte-dofus')
			) {
				// existing translations
				replaceTextContent('Serveur', 'Server');
				replaceTextContent('Email de contact:', 'Contact email:');
				replaceTextContent('Nom du personnage:', 'Character name:');
				replaceTextContent('Nom Complet', 'Full name');
				replaceTextContent('Mode de paiements:', 'Payment methods:');
				replaceTextContent('Binance (Id de paiement ou Email)', 'Binance (Payment id or Email)');
				replaceTextContent('Adresse de paiement', 'Payment Email');
				replaceTextContent('Adresse de crypto:', 'Crypto address:');
				replaceTextContent('Quantite :', 'Quantity:');
				replaceTextContent('Moyen de contact', 'Contact');
				replaceTextContent('Prix du million:', 'Price per million:');
				replaceTextContent('Vous devez être connecté pour vendre', 'You have to be logged in to sell');
				replaceTextContent('Vendre', 'Sell');
				replaceTextContent('Server du depart:', 'Original server:');
				replaceTextContent('Quantité à payer(Million):', 'Amount to pay (Million):');
				replaceTextContent('Personnage donneur:', 'Giving character:');
				replaceTextContent('Server d'arrivée:', 'New server:');
				replaceTextContent('Quantité à recevoir(Million):', 'Amount to receive (Million):');
				replaceTextContent('Vous devez être connecté pour échanger', 'You have to be logged in to trade');
				replaceTextContent('Personnage recepteur:', 'Receiving character:');
				replaceTextContent('Envoyer', 'Send');
				replaceTextContent('Reseau', 'Network');
				replaceTextContent('Choisis une quantite plus que', 'Choose an amount more than');

				// new translations for /vendre-compte-dofus
				replaceTextContent('Jeux', 'Games');
				replaceTextContent('Serveur', 'Server');               // already above, but safe to repeat
				replaceTextContent('Niveau', 'Level');
				replaceTextContent('Classe', 'Class');
				replaceTextContent('sur', 'on');
				replaceTextContent('Nous avons besoin de', 'We need');
				replaceTextContent('Quantite de compte', 'Account quantity');
				replaceTextContent('Details des comptes', 'Account details');
				replaceTextContent(
				  'Nom du compte (ou email du compte)',
				  'Username or email address'
				);
				replaceTextContent('Mot de passe du compte', 'Account password');
				replaceTextContent('Ajouter', 'Add');
				replaceTextContent('Supprimeer', 'Delete');
				replaceTextContent('Multicompte', 'Multi‑account');
				replaceTextContent('Monocompte', 'Single‑account');
				replaceTextContent('Tous les serveurs', 'All servers');

        <script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
        
        const rate = 0.85852;
        
        // Sélecteurs des zones qui changent quand on filtre (Admin et Vendeur)
        const targetContainers = ['#sellerAccountsContainer', '#ankamaAdminAccountsContainer'];

        // Fonction utilitaire : Convertir et Formater
        function getEuroHtml(amount) {
            let eur = (amount * rate).toFixed(2);
            return '<span class="eur-est" style="display:block; font-size:0.85em; color:#888; font-weight:normal; margin-top:2px;">≈ ' + eur + ' €</span>';
        }

        // --- FONCTION PRINCIPALE DE MISE A JOUR ---
        function applyCurrencyConversion() {
            
            // A. KPIs (DASHBOARD)
            $('.kpi-card').each(function() {
                if ($(this).find('.eur-est').length > 0) return; // Déjà fait

                let label = $(this).find('.kpi-label').text().toLowerCase();
                let valueEl = $(this).find('.kpi-value');
                let txt = valueEl.text().trim();
                let val = parseFloat(txt.replace(/[^\d\.]/g, ''));

                let moneyKeywords = ['gains', 'solde', 'disponible', 'balance', 'wallet', 'earnings', 'revenu', 'montant', 'amount', 'price'];
                let excludedKeywords = ['accounts', 'comptes', 'verified', 'vérifiés', 'stock', 'deposited', 'déposés', 'total paid', 'payés', 'paid', 'pending', 'attente'];

                let isMoney = moneyKeywords.some(keyword => label.includes(keyword));
                let isExcluded = excludedKeywords.some(keyword => label.includes(keyword));

                if (isMoney && !isExcluded && $.isNumeric(val) && txt.indexOf('USD') === -1) {
                    valueEl.html(val + ' USD ' + getEuroHtml(val));
                }
            });

            // B. TABLEAUX (COLONNES PRIX)
            $('table').each(function() {
                let table = $(this);
                let priceColIndices = [];
                
                table.find('th').each(function(index) {
                    let headerText = $(this).text().toLowerCase();
                    if (headerText.includes('prix') || headerText.includes('price') || headerText.includes('montant') || headerText.includes('amount')) {
                        priceColIndices.push(index);
                    }
                });

                if (priceColIndices.length > 0) {
                    table.find('tr').each(function() {
                        let row = $(this);
                        priceColIndices.forEach(function(colIndex) {
                            let cell = row.find('td').eq(colIndex);
                            if (cell.find('.eur-est').length > 0) return; // Déjà fait

                            let txt = cell.text().trim();
                            let val = parseFloat(txt.replace(/[^\d\.]/g, ''));

                            if (!isNaN(val) && txt.indexOf('USD') === -1 && val > 0) {
                                cell.html('<span style="font-weight:bold;">' + val + ' USD</span>' + getEuroHtml(val));
                            }
                        });
                    });
                }
            });

            // C. RECAP FORMULAIRE PAIEMENT
            if ($('.ankama-rate-info').length === 0) {
                let fundsText = $('.available-funds, .wallet-balance').first().text();
                if (!fundsText) {
                     $('.kpi-card').each(function() {
                        let l = $(this).find('.kpi-label').text().toLowerCase();
                        if (l.includes('disponible') || l.includes('solde') || l.includes('wallet') || l.includes('balance')) {
                            fundsText = $(this).find('.kpi-value').text(); 
                        }
                    });
                }
                if (fundsText) {
                    let val = parseFloat(fundsText.replace(/[^\d\.]/g, ''));
                    if (val > 0) {
                        let msg = '<div class="ankama-rate-info" style="margin-top:5px; font-size:0.9em; color:#666;">Taux du jour : 1 USD = '+rate+' EUR</div>';
                        $('#payout_method').after(msg);
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // --- OBSERVATEUR DE CHANGEMENTS (La solution miracle) ---
        // Cet observateur surveille les conteneurs et relance le script quand le HTML change
        const observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
            // On désactive temporairement l'observateur pour éviter une boucle infinie (car on va modifier le DOM nous-mêmes)
            observer.disconnect();
            
            // On applique les devises
            applyCurrencyConversion();
            
            // On réactive l'observateur
            startObserving();
        });

        function startObserving() {
            targetContainers.forEach(function(id) {
                let target = document.querySelector(id);
                if (target) {
                    observer.observe(target, { childList: true, subtree: true });
                }
            });
        }

        // 1. Exécution initiale
        applyCurrencyConversion();
        
        // 2. Lancement de la surveillance
        startObserving();

    });
    </script>

        <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

        var messages = {
            fr: { warning: 'Minimum : ', button: '⚠️ Minimum requis : ' },
            en: { warning: 'Min: ',      button: '⚠️ Minimum required: ' },
            es: { warning: 'Mínimo: ',   button: '⚠️ Mínimo requerido: ' },
            pt: { warning: 'Mínimo: ',   button: '⚠️ Mínimo necessário: ' }
        };

        function getLang() {
            var path = window.location.pathname;
            if (path.indexOf('/eng') !== -1) return 'en';
            if (path.indexOf('/es') !== -1)  return 'es';
            if (path.indexOf('/pt') !== -1)  return 'pt';
            return 'fr';
        }

        var lang        = getLang();
        var hasTyped    = false;
        var originalBtn = $('.frm_button_submit.frm_final_submit').text();

        function isMobile() {
            return $(window).width() <= 768;
        }

        $('#frm_field_164_container').css('position', 'relative');

        // Inject warning span — after the input group (works for both positions)
        $('#field_d4gzv').closest('.frm_input_group').after(
            '<span id="custom-min-warning" style="' +
                'display:none;' +
                'color:#c0392b;' +
                'font-size:0.82em;' +
                'white-space:nowrap;' +
                'font-weight:500;' +
            '"></span>'
        );

        function positionWarning() {
            var $group   = $('#field_d4gzv').closest('.frm_input_group');
            var $warning = $('#custom-min-warning');

            if (isMobile()) {
                // Below the field, no absolute positioning
                $warning.css({
                    position   : 'static',
                    display    : 'block',
                    marginTop  : '6px',
                    transform  : 'none',
                    left       : 'auto',
                    top        : 'auto'
                });
            } else {
                // To the right, absolute
                var left = $group.position().left + $group.outerWidth() + 12;
                var top  = $group.position().top + $group.outerHeight() / 2;
                $warning.css({
                    position  : 'absolute',
                    display   : 'inline',
                    marginTop : '0',
                    transform : 'translateY(-50%)',
                    left      : left + 'px',
                    top       : top + 'px'
                });
            }
        }

        function checkMinimum() {
            if (!hasTyped) return;

            var $field   = $('#field_d4gzv');
            var rawVal   = $field.attr('data-raw-value') || $field.val();
            var value    = parseFloat(rawVal) || 0;
            var minimum  = parseFloat($('#field_ibz2m').val()) || 0;
            var $btn     = $('.frm_button_submit.frm_final_submit');
            var $warning = $('#custom-min-warning');

            if (rawVal !== '' && value < minimum) {
                $warning.html('⚠️ ' + messages[lang].warning + '<strong>' + minimum + '</strong>');
                positionWarning();
                $warning.show();

                $btn
                    .prop('disabled', true)
                    .css({ 'opacity': '0.7', 'cursor': 'not-allowed' })
                    .text(messages[lang].button + minimum + ' millions');

            } else {
                $warning.hide();

                $btn
                    .prop('disabled', false)
                    .css({ 'opacity': '1', 'cursor': 'pointer' })
                    .text(originalBtn);
            }
        }

        $('#field_d4gzv').on('input keyup change', function() {
            hasTyped = true;
            checkMinimum();
        });

        $('#field_ibz2m').on('input change', function() {
            if (hasTyped) checkMinimum();
        });

        // Reposition if window resizes (e.g. rotating phone)
        $(window).on('resize', function() {
            if ($('#custom-min-warning').is(':visible')) {
                positionWarning();
            }
        });

    });
    </script>
        <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
        var messages = {
            fr: { usd: 'Minimum : 20$', eur: 'Minimum : 20€' },
            en: { usd: 'Minimum: $20',  eur: 'Minimum: €20'  },
            es: { usd: 'Mínimo: 20$',   eur: 'Mínimo: 20€'   },
            pt: { usd: 'Mínimo: 20$',   eur: 'Mínimo: 20€'   }
        };

        var exemptValues = [
            'Boune 2', 'Boune 3', 'Boune 4',
            'Allisteria 2', 'Allisteria 3',
            'Fallanster 2'
        ];

        function getLang() {
            var path = window.location.pathname;
            if (path.indexOf('/eng') !== -1) return 'en';
            if (path.indexOf('/es') !== -1)  return 'es';
            if (path.indexOf('/pt') !== -1)  return 'pt';
            return 'fr';
        }
        function getCurrency(text) {
            if (text.indexOf('€') !== -1) return 'eur';
            return 'usd';
        }
        function isExempt() {
            var val = $('#field_s0x5r').val() || '';
            return exemptValues.indexOf(val.trim()) !== -1;
        }

        var lang        = getLang();
        var totalFields = ['#field_ndbpq', '#field_v60nx', '#field_bw27s', '#field_x5387'];

        function checkTotal($input) {
            var $span = $input.closest('.frm_form_field').find('.frm_inline_total');
            if ($span.length === 0) return;

            // Si la valeur de s0x5r est exemptée, on remet la couleur normale et on sort
            if (isExempt()) {
                $span.css('color', '');
                return;
            }

            var rawText  = $span.text().trim();
            var currency = getCurrency(rawText);
            var numeric  = parseFloat(rawText.replace(/[^0-9.\-]/g, ''));
            if (isNaN(numeric) || numeric < 20) {
                $span.css('color', '#c0392b')
                     .data('original', $span.data('original') || rawText)
                     .text(messages[lang][currency]);
            } else {
                $span.css('color', '');
            }
        }
        function checkAll() {
            $.each(totalFields, function(i, selector) {
                var $input = $(selector);
                if ($input.length) checkTotal($input);
            });
        }

        // Run on load
        checkAll();

        // Watch all total spans for Formidable recalculations
        $.each(totalFields, function(i, selector) {
            var $input = $(selector);
            if (!$input.length) return;
            var $span = $input.closest('.frm_form_field').find('.frm_inline_total')[0];
            if (!$span) return;
            new MutationObserver(function() {
                checkTotal($input);
            }).observe($span, { childList: true, subtree: true, characterData: true });
        });

        // Also re-check on any field change (including s0x5r)
        $('form').on('input change', 'input, select', function() {
            setTimeout(checkAll, 150);
        });
    });
    </script>

					<script>
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>

    <script>
    (function () {
      console.log('[LC] starting…');

      // ============ CONFIG ============
      var GROUPS = { english: 2, french: 1, arabic: 3 };
      var ENABLED_PATHS = [
        /\/commandes?\/?$/,
        /\/commandes?-echange\/?$/
      ];
      var SERVER_COUNTRY = "FR";
      var USER = {"email":"","name":""};
      // =================================

      var path = window.location.pathname.toLowerCase();
      console.log('[LC] path =', path, '| country =', SERVER_COUNTRY || '(none)', '| user =', USER.email || '(guest)');

      if (!ENABLED_PATHS.some(function (re) { return re.test(path); })) {
        console.log('[LC] STOP: path not in trigger list');
        return;
      }

      function decideByUrl() {
        if (/^\/eng(\/|$)/.test(path))     return { group: GROUPS.english, lang: "en", source: "url:/eng" };
        if (/^\/fr(\/|$)/.test(path))      return { group: GROUPS.french,  lang: "fr", source: "url:/fr"  };
        if (/^\/(es|pt)(\/|$)/.test(path)) return { group: GROUPS.english, lang: "en", source: "url:/es-pt" };
        return { group: GROUPS.french, lang: "fr", source: "default" };
      }
      var decision = (SERVER_COUNTRY === "MA")
        ? { group: GROUPS.arabic, lang: "ar", source: "ip:MA" }
        : decideByUrl();
      console.log('[LC] decision:', decision);

      // Wait for the LiveChat plugin's widget to be ready
      var attempts = 0;
      var poll = setInterval(function () {
        attempts++;
        if (window.LiveChatWidget && typeof window.LiveChatWidget.on === 'function') {
          clearInterval(poll);
          console.log('[LC] LiveChatWidget detected after ' + attempts + ' polls');
          attachToWidget(decision);
        } else if (attempts >= 100) {
          clearInterval(poll);
          console.warn('[LC] gave up waiting for LiveChatWidget after 10s');
        }
      }, 100);

      function attachToWidget(d) {
        var alreadyReady = false;
        try {
          var s = window.LiveChatWidget.get && window.LiveChatWidget.get('state');
          if (s) { alreadyReady = true; console.log('[LC] widget already ready, state =', s); }
        } catch (e) { /* not ready yet */ }

        if (alreadyReady) {
          configure(d);
        } else {
          window.LiveChatWidget.on('ready', function () {
            console.log('[LC] ✓ ready event fired');
            configure(d);
          });
        }
      }

      function configure(d) {
        var params  = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        var orderId = params.get('order') || '';

        // 1) Identify the visitor (passes name + email to LiveChat)
        try {
          if (USER.name)  window.LiveChatWidget.call('set_customer_name',  USER.name);
          if (USER.email) window.LiveChatWidget.call('set_customer_email', USER.email);
          console.log('[LC] customer identified:', USER.name, USER.email);
        } catch (e) { console.error('[LC] identify failed:', e); }

        // 2) Pass extra context as session variables (visible in agent's panel)
        try {
          window.LiveChatWidget.call('set_session_variables', {
            language:     d.lang,
            detected_via: d.source,
            page:         path,
            order_id:     orderId,
            url:          window.location.href,
            target_group: d.group
          });
          console.log('[LC] session variables set');
        } catch (e) { console.error('[LC] set_session_variables failed:', e); }

        // 3) Auto-open the widget
        try {
          window.LiveChatWidget.call('maximize');
          console.log('[LC] maximize() called');
        } catch (e) { console.error('[LC] maximize failed:', e); }
      }
    })();
    </script>

        // Get the source and destination fields
        const sourceField = $('#field_s0x5r');
        const destinationField = $('#field_q8esv');

        if (sourceField.length && destinationField.length) {
            if (sourceField.val() !== '') {

            destinationField.prop('readonly', true);

            return false; // Indicate failure
        }
    }

        }
    }, 500); // Check every 500ms

    <script>
    (function() {
        const CFG = {
            formId: '2',
            fieldId: '90',
            triggers: ["boune","fallanster","allisteria"],
            countdown: 5,
            timerText: 'Patientez'
        };
        
        let pendingBtn = null, timer = null, accepted = false, timerDone = false;
        
        const overlay = document.getElementById('frmWarnOverlay');
        const btnNo = document.getElementById('frmWarnNo');
        const btnYes = document.getElementById('frmWarnYes');
        const timerEl = document.getElementById('frmWarnTimer');
        const checkbox = document.getElementById('frmWarnAgree');
        
        function findField() {
            const id = CFG.fieldId;
            return document.querySelector('#field_' + id) ||
                   document.querySelector('select#field_' + id) ||
                   document.querySelector('[name="item_meta[' + id + ']"]') ||
                   document.querySelector('select[name="item_meta[' + id + ']"]') ||
                   document.querySelector('[id*="' + id + '"]');
        }
        
        function getVal() {
            const f = findField();
            if (!f) return '';
            if (f.tagName === 'SELECT') {
                const o = f.options[f.selectedIndex];
                return o ? (o.text || o.value) : '';
            }
            if (f.type === 'radio') {
                const c = document.querySelector('[name="' + f.name + '"]:checked');
                return c ? c.value : '';
            }
            return f.value || '';
        }
        
        function shouldPopup(v) {
            if (!v) return false;
            const n = v.toLowerCase().trim();
            return CFG.triggers.some(t => n === t || n.includes(t));
        }
        
        function updateBtn() {
            if (timerDone && checkbox.checked) {
                btnYes.disabled = false;
                btnYes.classList.add('on');
            } else {
                btnYes.disabled = true;
                btnYes.classList.remove('on');
            }
        }
        
        function show() {
            accepted = false;
            timerDone = false;
            checkbox.checked = false;
            timerEl.classList.remove('hidden');
            overlay.classList.add('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            updateBtn();
            startTimer();
        }
        
        function hide() {
            overlay.classList.remove('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
            if (timer) clearInterval(timer);
        }
        
        function startTimer() {
            let s = CFG.countdown;
            timerEl.innerHTML = CFG.timerText + ' <span id="frmWarnCount">' + s + '</span>s';
            
            timer = setInterval(function() {
                s--;
                const el = document.getElementById('frmWarnCount');
                if (el) el.textContent = s;
                if (s <= 0) {
                    clearInterval(timer);
                    timerDone = true;
                    timerEl.classList.add('hidden');
                    updateBtn();
                }
            }, 1000);
        }
        
        checkbox.addEventListener('change', updateBtn);
        
        function hookBtns() {
            document.querySelectorAll('form').forEach(form => {
                const fid = form.querySelector('input[name="form_id"]');
                if (!fid || fid.value !== CFG.formId) return;
                
                form.querySelectorAll('button[type="submit"], input[type="submit"], .frm_button_submit, .frm_submit button').forEach(btn => {
                    if (btn.dataset.frmHooked) return;
                    btn.dataset.frmHooked = '1';
                    
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        if (accepted) {
                            accepted = false;
                            return true;
                        }
                        if (shouldPopup(getVal())) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                            pendingBtn = btn;
                            show();
                            return false;
                        }
                    }, true);
                });
            });
        }
        
        btnNo.onclick = function() { hide(); pendingBtn = null; };
        
        btnYes.onclick = function() {
            if (this.disabled) return;
            hide();
            accepted = true;
            if (pendingBtn) {
                setTimeout(function() { pendingBtn.click(); }, 50);
            }
        };
        
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Escape' && overlay.classList.contains('active')) {
                hide();
                pendingBtn = null;
            }
        });
        
        function init() { hookBtns(); }
        
        if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
        } else {
            init();
        }
        setTimeout(init, 1000);
        setTimeout(init, 2500);
        
        if (typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
            jQuery(document).on('frmFormComplete frmPageChanged', function() {
                setTimeout(init, 300);
            });
        }
    })();
    </script>
